name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:King Deluxe Room
info:Stayed in May 2022
info:Solo travelers
info:2 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted May 29, 2022
msg:This is an ok hotel. Staff is kind and relatively English-friendly, but there is a wait for everything. The hotel layout is confusing-it is hard to find restrooms in public places, and there are 2 sets of elevators-one that will take you to a room and one that will not. Food is excellent, and is a highlight. 

Rooms are decent, but a little confusing and fancy. There are multiple sets of lights, for example, and it is hard to determine where to turn the lights on for different things. The toilet is automatic and is a little loud and creepy. While the room was clean-there were many signs of poor construction and wear and tear-stains on the washroom floor, cracks in a sink. I had to fill the bathtub up with the shower nozzle because the faucet for the tub was too far away from the wall and made the floor, not the tub, wet. I could not get the light on the table to turn on.

I wouldn't say this is a bad place, but for the high price I expect far, far better.

In fact, what makes customers feel the worst is attitude. Of course, attitude is relative to subjective behavior. I only make statements. I have my own problems, but as a well-run hotel I am sure there are more secure solutions. My girlfriend is a teacher from Shenzhen University, and she needs to report to the school and three-day inspection when entering and leaving Shenzhen. In order to let the driver open the room without any hassle, we checked in and entered the room in this way around 10 o'clock in the evening.

It is very understandable for the hotel's request, but only questioned the attitude of this hotel. As a high-end Hilton brand, Conrad is not a business or express hotel. I think it's entirely possible to have a more friendly attitude, rather than a blunt mechanical trea**ent on the opposite side of the customer. We are in-house guests and not employees under your jurisdiction. attitude decides everything.

All of the above can be understood as emotional issues, which have nothing to do with the hotel's cooperation with the epidemic, but only about attitude. Why do you let customers write hundreds of words in the middle of the night so they can't sleep? I think all the friends who will be staying should also be able to judge. The benevolent sees benevolence, and the wise sees wisdom. The star standard of the hotel is not only about the hardware, but also the service means, process, attitude and software settings.
